Hello! In this narrative you will be asked a series of questions that will determine your personal values. The assesment results are based on Schwart'z theory of basic values which assesses 10 universal personal beliefs in life. These include (text-colour:red)[benevolence, universalism, self- direction, achievement, stimulation, hedonism, security, conformity, tradition, and power] At the end you will be presented with a AI generated image that shows you how your designated value/belief can manifest itself in the real world.
